CREATE TABLE T_FILM_FLM
(
FLM_ID             INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
FLM_TITRE          VARCHAR(64),
FLM_REALISATEUR    VARCHAR(32),
FLM_DUREE_MN       SMALLINT,          
FLM_ANNEE          SMALLINT,
FLM_GENRE          VARCHAR(20)
);
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE T_SEANCE_SNC
(
 SNC_ID      INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
 FLM_ID      INT NOT NULL
             REFERENCES T_FILM_FLM (FLM_ID),
 SNC_DATE    DATE NOT NULL,
 SNC_HEURE   TIME NOT NULL,
 SNC_BILLET  SMALLINT DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL ,
 SNC_TARIF   DECIMAL(5,2) NOT NULL
);
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
